<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the select package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> select</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/select&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>These are the key exports:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> - Creates a <a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px" href="/overview/collection">collection interface</a> from an
array of items.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property to set the initial value of the select.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> property must be an array of strings. If selecting a single value,
pass an array with a single string.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">items</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">label</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Ghana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;gh&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">label</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Kenya&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;ke&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;ng&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selecting-multiple-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selecting multiple values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selecting-multiple-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow selecting multiple values.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">multiple</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-select-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled select value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-select-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> for controlled selection.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="using-a-custom-object-format" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using a custom object format<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-a-custom-object-format"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the select collection expects an array of items with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">label</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> properties. To use a custom object format, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToString</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToValue</code> properties to the collection function.</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToString</code> — A function that returns the string representation of an item.
Used to compare items when filtering.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToValue</code> — A function that returns the unique value of an item.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToDisabled</code> — A function that returns the disabled state of an item.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">groupBy</code> — A function that returns the group of an item.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">groupSort</code> — An array or function to sort the groups.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="usage-within-a-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within a form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-a-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use select in a form, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> and render <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getHiddenSelectProps()</code>.</p>

<h3 id="browser-autofill-support" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Browser autofill support<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#browser-autofill-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To support browser autofill for form fields like state or province, set
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoComplete</code> on the machine.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;state&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoComplete</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;address-level1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-an-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling an item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-an-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable a select item, use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToDisabled</code> in the collection.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">items</span><span class="token operator">:</span> countries<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">itemToDisabled</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">disabled</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="close-on-select" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Close on select<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#close-on-select"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the menu closes when you select an item with pointer, space, or
enter. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to keep it open.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnSelect</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-selection-control" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic selection control<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-selection-control"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the API for imperative updates.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">selectValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;ng&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h3 id="allowing-deselection-in-single-select-mode" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing deselection in single-select mode<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-deselection-in-single-select-mode"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h3 id="listening-for-open-and-close-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for open and close events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-open-and-close-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> to listen for open and close events.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean, value: string[] }</span>

<h3 id="grouping-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Grouping items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#grouping-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The select relies on the collection, so rendered items must match collection
items.</p>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">groupBy</code> on the collection to define item groups.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> select<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">itemToValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">itemToString</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">label</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">groupBy</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">group</span> <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">&quot;default&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Then, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection.group()</code> method to render the grouped items.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">group</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>group<span class="token punctuation">,</span> items<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> index<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>

<h3 id="usage-with-large-data" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage with large data<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-with-large-data"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>For large lists, combine select with a virtualization library like
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">react-window</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">@tanstack/react-virtual</code>.</p>

<h3 id="usage-within-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using select in a dialog, avoid rendering it in a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Portal</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Teleport</code>
outside the dialog focus scope.</p>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each select part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the select is open, the trigger and content is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selected-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Items are given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute, indicating whether they are selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;checked|unchecked&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for selected or unselected state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="highlighted-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for highlighted state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the select is invalid, the label and trigger is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the select is disabled, the trigger and label is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled select state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled label state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled option state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Optionally, when an item is disabled, it is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="empty-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Empty state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#empty-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When no option is selected, the trigger is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-placeholder-shown</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-placeholder-shown</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for empty select state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The select machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">ListCollection&lt;T&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The item collection</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; content: string; control: string; trigger: string; clearTrigger: string; label: string; hiddenSelect: string; positioner: string; item: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; itemGroup: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; itemGroupLabel: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the select. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The `name` attribute of the underlying select.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the underlying select.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoComplete</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The autocomplete attribute for the hidden select. Enables browser autofill (e.g. &quot;address-level1&quot; for state).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the select is read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the highlighted value of the select.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to loop the keyboard navigation through the options</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow multiple selection</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the select menu is open</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the select&#x27;s open state is controlled by the user</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToIndexFn</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ScrollToIndexDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to scroll to a specific index</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">composite</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the select is a composed with other composite widgets like tabs or combobox</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">deselectable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the value can be cleared by clicking the selected item.

bdr_3px">--available-width</kbd></div><span>The available width in viewport</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/listbox" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">ListBox WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Space</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the select and focuses the first selected item.<br />When focus is on the content, selects the highlighted item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the select and focuses the first selected item.<br />When focus is on content, selects the focused item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the select.<br />When focus is on content, moves focus to the next item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the select.<br />When focus is on content, moves focus to the previous item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Esc</kbd></div><div><span>Closes the select and moves focus to trigger.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">A-Z</kbd><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">a-z</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, selects the item whose label starts with the typed character.<br />When focus is on the listbox, moves focus to the next item with a label that starts with the typed character.</span></div></li></ul><a state\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports form submission and browser autofill\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the select package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"select/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the select anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"select\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the select package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as select from \"@zag-js/select\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the key exports:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecollection\u003c/code\u003e - Creates a \u003ca href=\"/overview/collection\"\u003ecollection interface\u003c/a\u003e from an\narray of items.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"select/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e property to set the initial value of the select.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e property must be an array of strings. If selecting a single value,\npass an array with a single string.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{13}\"\u003econst collection = select.collection({\n  items: [\n    { label: \"Nigeria\", value: \"ng\" },\n    { label: \"Ghana\", value: \"gh\" },\n    { label: \"Kenya\", value: \"ke\" },\n    //...\n  ],\n})\n\nconst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultValue: [\"ng\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelecting multiple values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to allow selecting multiple values.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{5}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  multiple: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled select value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e for controlled selection.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing a custom object format\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the select collection expects an array of items with \u003ccode\u003elabel\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e properties. To use a custom object format, pass the \u003ccode\u003eitemToString\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003eitemToValue\u003c/code\u003e properties to the collection function.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToString\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the string representation of an item.\nUsed to compare items when filtering.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToValue\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the unique value of an item.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToDisabled\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the disabled state of an item.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egroupBy\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the group of an item.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egroupSort\u003c/code\u003e — An array or function to sort the groups.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst collection = select.collection({\n  // custom object format\n  items: [\n    { id: 1, fruit: \"Banana\", available: true, quantity: 10 },\n    { id: 2, fruit: \"Apple\", available: false, quantity: 5 },\n    { id: 3, fruit: \"Orange\", available: true, quantity: 3 },\n    //...\n  ],\n  // convert item to string\n  itemToString(item) {\n    return item.fruit\n  },\n  // convert item to value\n  itemToValue(item) {\n    return item.id\n  },\n  // convert item to disabled state\n  itemToDisabled(item) {\n    return !item.available || item.quantity === 0\n  },\n  groupBy(item) {\n    return item.available ? \"available\" : \"unavailable\"\n  },\n  groupSort: [\"available\", \"unavailable\"],\n})\n\n// use the collection\nconst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within a form\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use select in a form, set \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e and render \u003ccode\u003eapi.getHiddenSelectProps()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"select/usage-with-form.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eBrowser autofill support\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo support browser autofill for form fields like state or province, set\n\u003ccode\u003eautoComplete\u003c/code\u003e on the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  name: \"state\",\n  autoComplete: \"address-level1\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling an item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable a select item, use \u003ccode\u003eitemToDisabled\u003c/code\u003e in the collection.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3-4}\"\u003econst collection = select.collection({\n  items: countries,\n  itemToDisabled(item) {\n    return item.disabled\n  },\n})\n\nconst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClose on select\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the menu closes when you select an item with pointer, space, or\nenter. Set \u003ccode\u003ecloseOnSelect\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to keep it open.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eProgrammatic selection control\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the API for imperative updates.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eapi.selectValue(\"ng\")\napi.setValue([\"ng\", \"ke\"])\napi.clearValue() // or api.clearValue(\"ng\")\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling open state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eopen\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e for controlled open state, or \u003ccode\u003edefaultOpen\u003c/code\u003e for\nuncontrolled initial state.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    setOpen(details.open)\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean, value: string[] }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling highlighted item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003ehighlightedValue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonHighlightChange\u003c/code\u003e to manage item highlight.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  highlightedValue,\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    setHighlightedValue(details.highlightedValue)\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue, highlightedItem, highlightedIndex }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003ePositioning the popup\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003epositioning\u003c/code\u003e to control popup placement and behavior.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  positioning: { placement: \"bottom-start\" },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eLooping the keyboard navigation\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, arrow key navigation stops at the first and last options. Set\n\u003ccode\u003eloopFocus: true\u003c/code\u003e to loop back around.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  loopFocus: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAllowing deselection in single-select mode\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edeselectable\u003c/code\u003e to allow clicking the selected item again to clear the value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  deselectable: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for highlight changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonHighlightChange\u003c/code\u003e to listen for highlighted item changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue, highlightedItem, highlightedIndex }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for selection changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to listen for selected item changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[], items: Item[] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for item selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonSelect\u003c/code\u003e when you need the selected item value immediately.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onSelect(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for open and close events\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e to listen for open and close events.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean, value: string[] }\n    console.log(details.open)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eGrouping items\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe select relies on the collection, so rendered items must match collection\nitems.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003egroupBy\u003c/code\u003e on the collection to define item groups.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst collection = select.collection({\n  items: [],\n  itemToValue: (item) =\u003e item.value,\n  itemToString: (item) =\u003e item.label,\n  groupBy: (item) =\u003e item.group || \"default\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen, use the \u003ccode\u003ecollection.group()\u003c/code\u003e method to render the grouped items.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e{\n  collection.group().map(([group, items], index) =\u003e (\n    \u0026#x3C;div key={`${group}-${index}`}\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getItemGroupProps({ id: group })}\u003e{group}\u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n      {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n        \u0026#x3C;div key={`${item.value}-${index}`} {...api.getItemProps({ item })}\u003e\n          \u0026#x3C;span {...api.getItemTextProps({ item })}\u003e{item.label}\u0026#x3C;/span\u003e\n          \u0026#x3C;span {...api.getItemIndicatorProps({ item })}\u003e✓\u0026#x3C;/span\u003e\n        \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n  ))\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage with large data\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor large lists, combine select with a virtualization library like\n\u003ccode\u003ereact-window\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e@tanstack/react-virtual\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eExample with \u003ccode\u003e@tanstack/react-virtual\u003c/code\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003efunction Demo() {\n  const selectData = []\n\n  const contentRef = useRef(null)\n\n  const rowVirtualizer = useVirtualizer({\n    count: selectData.length,\n    getScrollElement: () =\u003e contentRef.current,\n    estimateSize: () =\u003e 32,\n  })\n\n  const service = useMachine(select.machine, {\n    id: useId(),\n    collection,\n    scrollToIndexFn(details) {\n      rowVirtualizer.scrollToIndex(details.index, {\n        align: \"center\",\n        behavior: \"auto\",\n      })\n    },\n  })\n\n  const api = select.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  return (\n    \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getRootProps()}\u003e\n      {/* ... */}\n      \u0026#x3C;Portal\u003e\n        \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getPositionerProps()}\u003e\n          \u0026#x3C;div ref={contentRef} {...api.getContentProps()}\u003e\n            \u0026#x3C;div\n              style={{\n                height: `${rowVirtualizer.getTotalSize()}px`,\n                width: \"100%\",\n                position: \"relative\",\n              }}\n            \u003e\n              {rowVirtualizer.getVirtualItems().map((virtualItem) =\u003e {\n                const item = selectData[virtualItem.index]\n                return (\n                  \u0026#x3C;div\n                    key={item.value}\n                    {...api.getItemProps({ item })}\n                    style={{\n                      position: \"absolute\",\n                      top: 0,\n                      left: 0,\n                      width: \"100%\",\n                      height: `${virtualItem.size}px`,\n                      transform: `translateY(${virtualItem.start}px)`,\n                      whiteSpace: \"nowrap\",\n                      overflow: \"hidden\",\n                      textOverflow: \"ellipsis\",\n                    }}\n                  \u003e\n                    \u0026#x3C;span\u003e{item.label}\u0026#x3C;/span\u003e\n                    \u0026#x3C;span {...api.getItemIndicatorProps({ item })}\u003e✓\u0026#x3C;/span\u003e\n                  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n                )\n              })}\n            \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n          \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n        \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;/Portal\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within dialog\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen using select in a dialog, avoid rendering it in a \u003ccode\u003ePortal\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eTeleport\u003c/code\u003e\noutside the dialog focus scope.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach select part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute you can target in CSS.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eOpen and closed state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the select is open, the trigger and content is given a \u003ccode\u003edata-state\u003c/code\u003e\nattribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelected state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eItems are given a \u003ccode\u003edata-state\u003c/code\u003e attribute, indicating whether they are selected.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"item\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for selected or unselected state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eHighlighted state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a\n\u003ccode\u003edata-highlighted\u003c/code\u003e attribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"item\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for highlighted state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eInvalid state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the select is invalid, the label and trigger is given a \u003ccode\u003edata-invalid\u003c/code\u003e\nattribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for invalid state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabled state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the select is disabled, the trigger and label is given a \u003ccode\u003edata-disabled\u003c/code\u003e\nattribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled select state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled label state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled option state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOptionally, when an item is disabled, it is given a \u003ccode\u003edata-disabled\u003c/code\u003e attribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eEmpty state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen no option is selected, the trigger is given a \u003ccode\u003edata-placeholder-shown\u003c/code\u003e\nattribute.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-placeholder-shown] {\n  /* styles for empty select state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eMethods and Properties\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eMachine Context\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe select machine exposes the following context properties:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccontexttable
